***поссорить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поссорить.html>поссо́рить</a> (31107)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ссо́рить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ssóritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поссорить.html>поссо́рить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">possóritʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ссо́рить</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to embroil <i>(with)</i>, to cause to quarrel <i>(with)</i></li></ol>

***пост.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пост.html>пост</a> (1502)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*postъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пост.html>пост</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">post</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пост.html>поста́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пост.html>посты́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пост.html>посто́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fast <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">period of restricted eating</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:великий.html>вели́кий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пост.html>пост</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">velikij <b>post</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Great Lent (<i>lit.</i> great <b>fast</b>)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пости́ться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">postítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постный.html>по́стный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">póstnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пост.html>пост</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">post</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пост.html>поста́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пост.html>посты́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пост.html>посто́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>post, office, appointment, position, job</li>
<li>picket, outpost, guard post, station</li></ol>

***поставить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поставить.html>поста́вить</a> (373)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ставить.html>ста́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поставить.html>поста́вить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">postávitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ставить.html>ста́вить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to put, to place, to set, to stand, to station</li>
<li>to apply, to put on (a compress)</li>
<li>to put on stage, to stage, to produce, to present (a play)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">gambling</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wager, to place a bet, to stake</li>
<li>to raise, to put (a question)</li>
<li>to deliver, to supply, to furnish, to market, to purvey
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поставлять.html>поставля́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">postavljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:постановить.html>постанови́ть</a> (15373)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">станови́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stanovítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постановить.html>постанови́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">postanovítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">постановля́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">постана́вливать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to decree, to enact, to decide, to resolve
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:постановить.html>постанови́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:большинство.html>большинство́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>голосо́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>postanovítʹ</b> bolʹšinstvóm golosóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to resolve by a majority of votes</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:постановить.html>постанови́ли</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:строка.html>строка́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:протокол.html>протоко́ле</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>postanovíli</b> (stroká v protokóle)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">resolved</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:постановка.html>постано́вка</a> (6677)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постановка.html>постано́вка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">postanóvka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постановка.html>постано́вки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постановка.html>постано́вки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постановка.html>постано́вок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">theater</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> staging, production</li>
<li>performance, play</li>
<li>raising, erection</li>
<li>organization, arrangement, setting
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:постановка.html>постано́вка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́са</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>postanóvka</b> voprósa</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">formulation of the question</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

***постареть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:постареть.html>постаре́ть</a> (8306)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стареть.html>старе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">starétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постареть.html>постаре́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">postarétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стареть.html>старе́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to grow old, to age, to advance in age</li></ol>

***постелить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:постелить.html>постели́ть</a> (11260)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стелить.html>стели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stelítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постелить.html>постели́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">postelítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стелить.html>стели́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spread, to lay, to make (<i>bed</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мама.html>ма́ма</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:постелить.html>посте́лет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:постель.html>посте́ль</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Máma <b>postélet</b> mne postélʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Mum is going to make a bed for me.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:постелить.html>посте́лем</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:линолеум.html>лино́леум</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kogdá <b>postélem</b> linóleum?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">When shall we put linoleum on?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">постла́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">postlátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:застлать.html>застла́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zastlátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:постель.html>посте́ль</a> (1439)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Analyzable as deverbal from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постелить.html>постели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">postelítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постель.html>посте́ль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">postélʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постель.html>посте́ли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постель.html>посте́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постель.html>посте́лей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bed (<i>a piece of furniture to sleep on</i>)</li>
<li>(<i>no plural</i>) bedding (<i>bedclothes</i>)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:постигаемый.html>постига́емый</a> (12319)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постигаемый.html>постига́емый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">postigájemyj</span>)
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постигнуть.html>пости́гнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">postígnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
